[维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告（2020年12月31日）第63期（共 1021人）（三）](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2020/12/2020123163-1021_30.html)
------

<div>
<p><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span></span></span></b></p><a name='more'></a><b>续上，第三部分</b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12pt;">：<b>（<span lang="EN-US">G</span>、<span lang="EN-US">H</span>、<span lang="EN-US">I</span>、<span lang="EN-US">J</span>、<span lang="EN-US">K</span>）</b></span><p></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">G.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高光成、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高国香、高洪伟、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高惠仙、高继萍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高建君、高锦标、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高金平</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高俊、高立娟、高连红、高文淑、高维平、高贤英、高小平、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高小娓、高清秀</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高智晟、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">葛素芬、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">戈觉平、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">格桑梅朵（藏）、格桑秀郎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">革命（哈萨克）、革振华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根敦伦珠（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">根托（藏）、根珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿潇男</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、耿宜敏、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">更敦扎巴（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宫宝美、宫文义、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 110.25pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">公华、公丕启、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">巩进军</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡嘎（藏）、贡觉尼玛（藏）、贡却才培（藏）、贡却卓玛（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龚鲭林、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">龚圣亮</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、龚月贵、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷明龙、谷秀华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">官忠基、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">关振林、桂敏海、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭成茹、郭春该、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭丹霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭洪伟、郭宏英、郭平珍、郭泉<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">、</b>郭秀云、郭延达、郭艳华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">果然、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高光成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东潍坊市昌乐县<span lang="EN-US">5</span>图街道办邱家河村法轮功学员。高光成曾在<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份，因修炼法轮功被判刑十年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年出狱。高光成在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，在昌乐县黄埠村讲法轮功时，被黄埠村周涛恶意举报，被昌乐城南派出所抓捕。城南派出所警察高玉柱带领着<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个警察强行抄家。当时因疫情期间各看守所都不收人，高玉柱从高光成手机上找到了他女儿的电话恐吓说，交<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元钱办取保候审手续，不办就送往监狱。他女儿害怕就好说歹说交了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元办理了取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东省潍坊市青州法院对高光成开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高国香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省德州市陵城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功以来，高国香屡遭迫害。她曾被抓捕九次、拘禁关押共九次（关押四次、拘禁五次）、骚扰三次、抄家七次、勒索三万二千六百余元，劳教迫害一次，判刑一次。她还经历过：照相、抽血、按手印、签字、打耳光、拽头发、罚跪、脚踢、辱骂、逼看污蔑法轮功的录像、精神洗脑、逼迫写所谓“三书”、奴役等多种形式迫害，给老人精神身体及家人造成无法弥补的伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她和法轮功学员董娟，在德城区所辖赵虎乡镇集市上法轮功资料时，被抓捕，被关押在德州看守所，并被抄家，被抄走法轮功经书等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，高国香老太太被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款二万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省东营市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营市东营区胜利派出所、东三路派出所、明月派出所、文汇派出所警察同时出动，商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽等法轮功学员被秘密绑架。商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽被劫持到东营市看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营区法院对商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽庭审，并判处：王子明<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，商兆香<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；张爱丽<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元。四人上诉到东营市中级法院中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。高洪伟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高惠仙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日生，原云南省昆明钢铁公司桥钢厂职工，后被非法开除公职。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续迫害中，高惠仙曾两次被中共判刑，共遭冤狱九年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日高惠仙向安宁市太平街道办事处龙箐村中共支部书记何顺贵讲法轮功真相，同时赠送了一本「明慧日历」向他祝福。结果何顺贵向公安机关诬告高惠仙。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日高惠仙正在母亲家里，被安宁市国保大队警察非法撬锁入室抓捕、抄家，警察抢走计算机、打印机、大法书籍、法轮功数据等大量私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被昆明市西山区法院判刑七年，罚款一千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高继萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高建君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高建君被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高锦标</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：男，河南省新密市公民，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因言获罪被行政拘留，随后又转为刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被正式逮捕。罪名是寻衅滋事。后法院以其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月在海外网站推特上“大量散布反对党和国家以及政府的言论、图片和视频”，严重损害国家形象和国家利益，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日将高锦标判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。高锦标不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，二审又维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高金平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，保定市依棉厂退休职工，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>中午，高金平在保定市满城区出租房内被保定市公安局国保警察和保定市竞秀区依棉派出所抓捕，并同时抢走电脑、大法书籍等个人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，高阳县法院对高金平开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，高金平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">高俊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，高俊、张永宝二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高立娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津石化公司青年女教师、法轮功学员。高立娟<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被当地警察绑架。高立娟遭构陷的案卷两次被检察院退回，办案单位大港胜利派出所及大港国继续罗列罪名，又把高立娟起诉到天津滨海新区法院，意欲高立娟重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日高立娟案在天津滨海新区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万。高丽娟上诉被驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高连红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省高密市拒城河社区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日高连红被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">高文淑：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，山东省青岛市城阳区流亭赵村人，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功而被青岛市当局多次绑架迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，高文淑和丈夫邵承洛在夏庄镇发法轮功宣传材料时，被当地治安人员告发，当场即被夏庄派出所警方以涉“邪教罪”抓走，其家被查抄四次，并且警方在没有出具任何凭据的情况下，劫走家里二万元现金及许多物品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，城阳区法院在城阳看守所内设法庭，高文淑和她的丈夫均被非法庭审，当庭未予宣判。之后，高文淑的家人为她聘请了律师，但律师向法官提出再次庭审要求时遭到拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇二人被山东青岛城阳区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别宣判，其被重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其丈夫被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。两人不服，均已提出上诉。目前被关押在青岛市城阳看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高维平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁、北京市东城区女法轮功学员、原中国新闻社研究部采编，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年修炼法轮法。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年中国大水灾，她默默拿出<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元支援灾区失学儿童。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月当局疯狂迫害法轮功后，高维平多次被非法拘留，两次被非法劳教，被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被侨办、中新社非法处分，扣发工资，无故开除，失去经济来源，并被迫与丈夫离婚，独身一人生活。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，高维平<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在北京王府井新华书店将真相书签放入书内，被书店经理诬告，后被东城区东方广场派出所数名警察绑架。东方广场派出所成立一个近十人的所谓“案件小组”，将高维平构陷到东城检察院。被构陷所谓“破坏法律实施<span lang="EN-US">300</span>条”，被关押在东城区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，法轮功学员高维平被东城区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚款八千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高贤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川泸州市合江县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。高贤英曾被非刑两次，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，四川泸州市七名法轮功学员高贤英、董国珍、周明英、张元华、刘忠芬、帅先芳、宋平（男）驱车到泸州市合江县五通镇赶场，被派出所警察抓捕，然后带到合江九支镇派出所审问。后因年纪大，回家监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院高显英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，处罚金七千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东潍坊市昌邑市法轮功学员，在中共对法轮功持续至今近<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的迫害中，被迫流离失所多年，落脚在聊城市东昌府区。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日与法轮功学员黄焕芝，在散发真相资料时，被李海务派出所警察抓捕，关押在聊城市看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日高小平被山东聊城法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，黄焕芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。两名善良妇女现已在山东女子监狱服刑。高小平刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高小娓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，农民，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆（洗脑班）至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被铐在铁椅子上<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天，臀部都坐烂了，后被关押在宝鸡市第二看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，宝鸡市金台区法院给下达起诉书及监视居住六个月通知。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高清秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省张家口市沽源县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，沽源县法轮功学员高清秀、孙润桃、赵梅在长梁乡顺路讲法轮功、免费传递法轮功法轮功资料时，遭人恶告，遭警方抓捕。孙润桃和高清秀<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，分别被张北县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。高清秀刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高智晟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，陕西省榆林市佳县人，著名维权律师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起，开始替弱势群体维权打官司，曾处理过多宗民间维权案件；自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底起，开始多次上书中共当局高层，要求改变对法轮功等群体的非法处理手段，并参与对法轮功学员器官遭当局活摘指控的调查；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，与妻子公开宣布退出中国共产党；因其勇于于为当局认定的敏感性案件（注：含法轮功信仰者、地下基督教徒以及与官员发生纠纷的底层农民和私营企业家）辩护，故而曾多次受到中共官方机构或组织（<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室）黑社会手段的严重骚扰和打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其执业执照被当局吊销，随后被秘密绑架并遭到约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日起其与外界失联，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月才被当局释放返京；后因其接受了美联社采访，遂被再次与外界失联，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其亲友才从新华社报导中得知，其缓刑已被北京法院撤销，须继续服刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日刑满出狱，此前在新疆维吾尔自治区沙雅监狱服刑。出狱后高智晟仍被严密监控，且不让治牙看病，致其因长期在狱中遭受酷刑折磨和被单独囚禁，迄今仍牙齿松动，身体健康欠佳；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在陕北老家秘密撰写的新书《<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，起来中国》在台湾正式印刷出售，因该书涉及中共当局对其长期绑架、囚禁和施以酷刑等，以及他从信仰角度看中共<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年将会灭亡和对<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年后的中国未来宪政民主化展望等三大内容，遂令当局十分恐惧、恼怒，对其监控愈加严密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬在老家失踪，后获知被当局控制带回北京关押。目前已遭强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多，音信全无，生死不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">葛素芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，葛素芬等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，葛素芬被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京市丰台区岳各庄的维权残疾人。住北京丰台区魏家村南<span lang="EN-US">20</span>号院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号楼门<span lang="EN-US">2</span>门<span lang="EN-US">1305</span>室。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，葛志慧和同区石榴庄东街<span lang="EN-US">195</span>号的被强拆人李美青，到达中央扫黑除恶督导组驻地反映政府的黑社会化强拆，结果在督导组驻地的门口，遭到丰台区副区长带队的维稳人员的阻截，求见扫黑除恶督导组未果。但是，没隔多久，葛志慧竟遭刑事拘留。罪名是寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，葛志慧被构陷案开庭，未当庭宣判。现被关押在丰台看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戈觉平</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：江苏苏州维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日戈觉平（网络名称：奔博）被苏州市公安局直属分局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住。戈觉平（奔博）、陆国英夫妇是癌症病患者，尤其是戈觉平，需要长期服中药，其身体状况令人担忧。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">戈觉平至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月已被超期羁押近两年，狱中身体状况不佳，一直高血压，现在每天要吃五颗降压药，平时都躺着休息。日前又传出其在看守所原病处有发炎、化脓症状，之前家属和律师曾多次向看守所提出取保申请，却一直未获批准。其妻陆国英反映，丈夫以前得过癌症，后做手术治愈，但需长期服中药，而看守所根本不具备熬药的条件，她现在非常担心丈夫的身体状况。希望看守所方面能尽快批准他的取保申请。到<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月仍未开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，苏州中院判处戈觉平煽动颠覆罪<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">格桑梅朵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨一小学女教师。格桑梅朵是第一位可以被知道的因翻墙而遭中共当局强迫失踪的藏人。据了解，格桑梅朵曾在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>上转发外媒 《自由亚洲电台》和《挪威西藏之声》中文部有关藏区的新闻报道，以促进使用<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>的中国网友，特别是她的汉族朋友们了解西藏问题的真相。梅朵非常了解西藏的历史和现实。格桑梅朵翻墙转发外媒西藏新闻一事被发现后，当局开始对她进行迫害，她所在的小学将梅朵开除，梅朵继而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年遭到当局强迫失踪，至今已下落不明<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现获悉，格桑梅朵被以“泄露国家秘密”定罪，关押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">格桑秀郎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达木寺僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后一直被秘密关押，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被拉萨市中级法院以“带领民众集会”罪名判处<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑。目前被关押在西藏拉萨的扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革命（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">他与叶尔波里（哈萨克）都是新疆伊犁州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县哈萨克族人，自由职业者，伊斯兰教信仰者，哈萨克族人权捍卫者。由于没有办理信教许可证（即未到当地政府部门申请批准），坚持自行做祷告，并经常到清真寺，因此于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月被抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬分别被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。据一位哈萨克同乡称，因他们都无正式职业，平时靠打散工或装修房子度日，二人家庭都十分贫困。被捕后，当地公安不准家属聘请律师，也拒绝向家属出示判决书。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革振华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">63</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区人，原阿城区低压电器厂职工，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年曾被哈尔滨市阿城市公安局非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。在哈尔滨市长林子劳教所期间，经常遭到警察和犯人的毒打，被强迫长时间坐小板凳等。因劳教所环境恶劣，他身上长满了疥疮，疼痛难忍。每天还要强迫他做十几个小时的苦役，完不成任务就罚站。其左肋骨曾被警察和犯人打断两根，但仍不放过他，逼他出工干活，一天也不许休息。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日凌晨，他在哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被当地警方闻讯赶来围捕、绑架，后被关押在尚志市看守所。与其一起的法轮功学员菽坤和王翠娥也遭抓捕，至今未归。因长期不知革振华的消息，其妻经多方打听，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才知道丈夫革振华已被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。据悉，革振华不服，提起上诉，但二审仍维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。目前服刑地不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根敦伦珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，青海藏族作家、诗人，曾是青海同仁县隆务寺僧人，过去曾数次被当局逮捕。同仁县熟悉此事的消息人士介绍，根敦伦珠对保护母语藏语文和西藏文化非常关心。他的作品在境内和流亡藏人拥有很大的影响力。根敦伦珠于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年十月在网站上发表了一首诗歌，内容是作家和艺术家需要有言论和思想不受限制的自由。尽管面临诸多限制，根敦伦珠仍坚持创作，并从其读者处获得支持。青海当局制订的藏区“扫黑除恶”政策中，把提倡“保护母语”视为黑恶势力行为。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，青海省黄南州藏族作家、诗人根敦伦珠被中共当局逮捕，关押至秘密地点，下落不明。据悉，当局在对其实施长时间监视后采取了这个行动。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根托（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根托，现年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根珠，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52140367"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿潇男：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52140367;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年代出生，出版人，独立电视制作人，文化企业家，传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司董事长，北京文化公共领域领军人物，公益文化思想活动策划<span lang="EN-US">/</span>执行<span lang="EN-US">/</span>传播者，中国在押政治犯。 耿潇男早年曾就读于中央戏剧学院，毕业后逐渐成为中国文化出版人，电影人，历任中国天画画天影业首席执行官、瑞雅书业总编辑，之后又和丈夫秦真共同创立传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司，并担任董事长，随在业界知名度较高；近年来，因在北京文化公共领域以活跃、敢言着称，并积极致力于公益文化思想活动策划、执行及传播活动等，遂遭北京当局的维稳监控打压；<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦真<span lang="EN-US">/</span>耿潇男夫妇二人突然被警方带走，随后被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌”非法经营罪“刑拘，现在北京市海淀区看守所关押；北京当局曾以经济问题为名调查其二人所属的出版公司，其丈夫与公司的账号均被查封；多名好友均称其被抓捕，恐与此前公开为多名中国公共知识分子及异见人士发声呼吁有关，乃是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月遭正式逮捕。 </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耿宜敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇环北七路<span lang="EN-US">47</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂会堂主任，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，该基督教会接到当地县政府发来的欲拆除教会通知，声称政府要对阜南县富陂大道西侧实施棚改项目，而其教堂因位于该项目征收范围，所以需要拆除；因政府仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称若要异地重建政府将不予相应补偿，面对此单方武断决策，其及牧师、众信徒们认为明显有失公允，故遭到包括其在教会众教友的坚决反对，遂遭当局恶意报复与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，当教堂众教友在做礼拜聚会时，突遭地方当局的强行闯入拆除，拆除时无任何合法文件及通知出示，且因事发突然，教堂财物来不及搬出，以致所有物品近都毁坏；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与教会牧师、部分会堂成员数人被阜南县警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原审，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">更敦扎巴（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁，四川省阿坝羌族藏族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇索藏村人，索克藏寺续部学院资深僧人和寺院办公室职员。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜里在自己僧舍里突遭一批不属于当地警方的国保警察野蛮抓捕。抓捕时，不仅没有说明理由，而且还使用暴力，用手铐铐住双手，用枪顶住脸部。此后长期失联，官方拒绝透露其被捕原因、关押地点及其身体状况等信息。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被四川阿坝羌族藏族自治州黑水县法院以“煽动分裂国家”、“非法联系境外”罪判处徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，关押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">宫宝美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">安徽省蚌埠市法轮功学员。安徽省宿州市灵璧县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及国保大队人员、蚌埠市<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及国保大队人员共十几人，在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，闯入家在蚌埠市禹会区一所居民楼法轮功学员宫宝美家，强行搜查，掠去几万元现金，据目击者说，打印机器及各种真相资料，装有几车运走。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，宫宝美被蚌埠市灵璧县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宫文义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了宫文义等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其他<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名法轮功学员被松北区检察院起诉。宫文义因身体原因保外回家，检察院称另案处理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，宫文义在哈尔滨市江北住处，警察再次抓捕，并被抄家。后被在哈市第一看守所关押。后宫文义于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被哈市道外区法院秘密开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被押送哈市呼兰监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">公华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省日照市法轮功学员，日照市裕华机械厂职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>两日，日照市公安局东港分局国保警察先后抓捕了法轮功学员公华、孙平、屈正蓉等八位学员，关押在日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日公华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">公丕启：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，山东省青岛市人，前山东省预备役高炮师副参谋长、退休上校、正团职军官，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年信仰、锻炼法轮功以来，深受中共当局的打压逼迫；曾因其家人及其本人均锻炼法轮功之故而被迫提前“退休”，并遭多次威胁，被当局用开除“党籍”、撤销职务及工资待遇、收回住房、开除孩子学籍、投入监狱等方式胁迫其放弃修炼；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾与妻子在家中被青岛市警方以邪教罪由拘捕，后其妻被枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，其虽未被判刑，但被关押在部队接受洗脑再教育，其女儿在外上学也因此断绝了生活来源，无家可归；关押期间，因拒绝放弃信仰而被长期关小屋，遭受酷刑虐待，直至在经历了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个半月的磨难之后才得以释放；因其坚持信仰不动摇，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，在去朋友家中串门之际再次被青岛市市北区警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘，家被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被转正式逮捕，并关押在青岛市即墨普东看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其案被青岛市市北区法院在青岛市即墨普东看守所内正式开庭，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其不服提起上诉，经青岛市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">巩进军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曾因房屋遭遇强拆而上访多年，并屡遭截访，被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因长期滞留北京上访，遂被送至黑监狱马家楼关押，后又被遣返原籍，途中其一行四人（均为访民）因遭到黑保安的非人虐待且拘不让饮食，故而在其人身自由及安全被“黑保安”非法严重侵害的情况下被迫予以正当防卫，双方发生激烈冲突，引发刺死黑保安事件（警方称一死一伤）；案发后河北省饶阳县警方迅速将其抓捕刑拘，并被关押在河北省衡水市深州看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被河北省衡水市中院以“故意伤害罪”判处无期徒刑；据悉其在被审讯时曾遭严重酷刑，仅一天即被电击<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次。目前在河北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡嘎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡藏民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早从<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，中国政府就开始计划将在拉萨市林周县附近的矿区建设、实施“旁多水利枢纽工程”。因该工程要在两条交汇于林周县旁多乡的河流——热振河、旁多措河之上筑坝截水，故为确保顺利开工，相关政府部门就于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召开藏民大会，郑告村民此工程是“中共中央的指令，若有藏人试图阻止施工，将以政治罪名进行拘捕”。随后几年，因有关部门迅速投入大量施工准备，不仅在当地做频繁测量、建桥及建路等工作，而且炸山挖石，大量采矿，随意排放污水，导致当地的自然生态环境出现严重毁坏，附近村民的民房出现裂痕及大面积农田被毁坏等现象。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因拉萨市林周县的“旁多水利枢纽工程”正式开工，当局随立即强迫旁多乡<span lang="EN-US">119</span>户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>名）藏民尽快整体搬迁。因当地藏民不愿搬迁，故而多次向政府部门提出投诉请求，但均毫无果效。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，遂被迫进行集体维权与和平请愿，以期能借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目。不料却遭到中共西藏当局的强烈打压。贡嘎、白玛等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名藏族人权捍卫者因此遭拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，贡嘎、白玛等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案分别被拉萨市法院以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由秘判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等徒刑，其亦被判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡觉尼玛（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州（以下简称阿坝州）若尔盖县人，西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺果芒学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期进入西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺的果芒学院对佛教进修、研读；后因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成其身边主要弟子，加之自身对佛学严谨博学的治学态度，故而被哲蚌寺果芒学院确立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因藏区发生大规模以僧侣为主体，要求中共当局实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁让达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求的抗议活动，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在寺庙约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧人亦积极参与其中，致使抗议活动态势迅速扩展到整个拉萨市区，以及四川、青海等藏区；针对此次抗议游行，中共西藏当局很快调拨大批持枪武警，因管控手段过于极端，遂导致双方发生对峙冲突，其间有不少僧人被抓捕，其余人等被送回寺庙严管看守；尽管此前其并未参加抗议游行活动，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“抗议活动”抓走刑拘，自此失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后其被拉萨市检察院正式批捕，理由是未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，其狱中具体境况等信息不明。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">贡却才培（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Kunchok Tsephel Gopey Tsang</span>，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州玛曲县欧拉乡人，曾担任玛曲县藏文中学英语教师，并任玛曲县畜牧局公务员、藏语及藏族网络作家和琼迈藏语文学网编辑，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年曾因涉嫌政治活动而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，后无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因在互联网上发表了与西藏<span lang="EN-US">3.14</span>事件有关的文章，同时向外界披露藏人在抗议事件中被镇压、军警抓捕寺院僧侣等消息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被从家中逮捕，并遭搜查，之后与外界失去联系；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被甘肃省甘南藏族自治州中级法院秘密审判，以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。先在甘肃省甘南自治州合作监狱服刑，后关押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡却卓玛（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因手中举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，在县城一处街道上和平游行，以此表达自己对达赖喇嘛尊者的崇敬，随立即被驻守在街道附近的中共警方拘捕。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">龚月贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，家住武穴市刊江办事处，目前被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。龚月贵刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龚鲭林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市仪陇县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，仪陇县金城镇派出所警察打电话给龚鲭林，让他把身份证拿去派出所登记一下。龚鲭林就拿着自己的身份证，去当地派出所登记，结果被警察抓捕。警察从龚鲭林身上强行搜去他家的钥匙，去他家抄家，警察非法抄走的龚鲭林的私人财物有：法轮功书籍、计算机、打印机等，现金八万多元。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，龚鲭林被庭审，并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">龚圣亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督教牧师，华南教案首犯。龚圣亮牧师是湖北省枣阳市人，华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）的创始人和领袖，该教派是中国一个家庭教会团契，在几个省份有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名信徒。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，龚圣亮在湖北省钟祥市被捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，他被湖北省荆门市中级法院裁定罪名成立，根据中国的反邪教法判处死刑。但由于国际压力，中国放弃了宗教罪名和死刑，并下令重新审判。中国湖北省高级法院后以事实不清、证据不足为由驳回了荆门市中级法院对基督教华南教会五名成员的死刑判决后，荆门市中级法院重新作出一审判决，把龚圣亮、徐福明、胡勇等三人改判无期徒刑，龚邦坤、李英改判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，原先在一审被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年徒刑的向凤屏和刘先知等四人获当庭释放。一些作证反对龚的人后来表示，他们遭到了残酷的刑讯逼供。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区人，原任职乌鲁木齐政府机关工作人员，网络作家，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件发生时用手机短信向境外担任挪威维吾尔协会副秘书长的丈夫拜合提亚尔联系<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多次通报看到的情况，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被新疆乌鲁木齐市警方逮捕，据称在拘留期间曾遭受酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威”罪判处无期徒刑。目前在乌鲁木齐水磨沟女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷明龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北保定市定州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，谷明龙因到高蓬镇钮店村发放法轮功资料被定州市公安局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底被定州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在唐山某监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷秀华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。谷秀华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">官忠基：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛市平度市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月平度市法院对法轮功学员官忠基判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，山东省青岛市法院又对官忠基上诉案维持原判。官忠基，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，山东省平度市东阁办事处后巷子村人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，平度市七、八个警察到青岛李沧官忠基的儿子家将官忠基绑架到平度市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">关振林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">甘肃省酒泉市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被甘肃省酒泉市警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被甘肃省酒泉市法院一审以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">桂敏海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，汉族，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，原籍中国宁波，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年加入瑞典国籍，“巨流传媒有限公司”股东。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月的中共特工赴香港、泰国实施的“香港铜锣湾书店案”震惊世界，共绑架了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人，分别是桂敏海、林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波。后此<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人都于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被中共逼迫在电视上认罪。桂敏海<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬在央视称自己是为<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年前在宁波醉驾撞死人事件而潜返中国投案自首；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桂敏海又在电视镜头前承认自己非法偷运禁书进入大陆。后林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波相继被释放，唯有桂敏海遭扣押。中共当局一度声称桂敏海取保获释，实际上是仍遭秘密关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被中共当局关押期间，中共称经其本人申请依法恢复中国国籍。宁波市中级法院于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日公开宣判，认定桂敏海犯为境外非法提供情报罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭成茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十四岁。郭成茹，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被天津市河西区桃园派出所警察抓捕、非法关押、构陷。这是继郭成茹过去的六次被抓捕、十二年冤狱后的第七次被抓捕。从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日这<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年间里，即从郭成茹三十五岁到四十九岁这段日子，她两次被非法劳教、两次被非法判刑、多次被非法拘留，累计<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年时间她是被囚禁在中共的看守所、劳教所、监狱中度过的。在对法轮功的灭绝政策下，她被多次野蛮灌食迫害，被酷刑吊铐折磨，被破坏中枢神经的药物迫害到一度失忆、失语、丧失认知、表达等能力，被警察包夹折磨到一度精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份家人得知，郭成茹已被河西区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚款五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭春该</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。目前此案音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭丹霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省岳阳市石油公司退休会计、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。郭丹霞是于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被岳阳市楼区公安分局国保大队多个警察入室抓捕、抄家、审讯，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被检察院批捕，六月份被关押到岳阳市康复医院（精神病医院）。后郭丹霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，处罚金五千元。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">郭洪伟：</span></b><a name="_Hlk54873666"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉林省四平市铁东区人</span></a><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">，人权捍卫者。原是吉林省白山市抚松县松江河发电厂职工，遭冤假错案报复陷害 ，入狱五年，逼迫上访十年至今未果。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被构陷涉嫌“寻衅滋事”遭逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，郭洪伟、肖蕴玲被“敲诈吉林市公安局”一案在吉林省四平市公安局铁东区法院开庭审理。羁押于吉林省四平市看守所。原定于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日开庭，当日家属接到通知要延期开庭，律师及家属寻人无果。后得知郭洪伟狱中遭遇酷刑，身体状况恶化被送医院。之后于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被吉林省四平市铁东区法院以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。狱中一直遭虐待，情况危殆。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭宏英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省四平市铁东区人。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日是替母亲肖蕴苓、哥哥郭洪伟进京伸冤，而在“两会”期间被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天的郭宏英女士获释的日子，郭宏英的八旬老父亲拖着病体到拘留所，结果眼睁睁看着女儿被四平市铁东区分局南四纬派出所的从截走，得到的是一张由行政拘留改为刑事拘留的家属通知书。郭宏英哥哥郭洪伟原是国企中层干部，因秉公管理得罪了某同事，被其在检察院的亲属报复构陷入狱五年，因此而走上了血泪上访路。上访过程中，为了维持生计，承包了个小诊所，经营刚有起色却遭到违约，且由公安违法参与民事纠纷，造成巨大的经济损失。真是福无双至祸不单行。痛上痛冤上冤把郭洪伟几尽逼上了绝路，逐渐悟出了信访是骗局，是在用时间杀害上访人，携年迈父母进京上访遭到地方政府以敲诈政府公安罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，其<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的老母亲也判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。郭洪伟坐着轮椅，患高危三级高血压服刑，其母肖蕴苓多病缠身高龄服刑。服刑其间母子二人多次出现病危，当局不允许保外就医，有将母子二人冤死狱中的嫌疑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：吉林四平公民郭宏英涉嫌寻衅滋事、妨害公务案四平市铁东区法院判决书已经下达，郭宏英被以寻衅滋事罪判决<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，妨碍公务罪判决<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，执行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭平珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，家住武穴市田镇，美容院老板，目前被非法关押在蕲春县拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，郭平珍被取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，郭平珍在流亡中被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。郭平珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭泉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，江苏省南京市人，原南京师范大学副教授、研究生导师，中国大陆新民党创始人及代理主席，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年曾因发表公开信要求中国进行宪政改革，宣布组建“中国新民党”，主张在中国实行多党制和军队国家化等，遭受到中共当局的打压，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被南京师范大学党委以违反宪法和教师法为由撤销其副教授职务，调任数据员；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又因撰文批评中国政府处理四川地震的方式不当而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，再次因其在网上发表<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多篇名为《民主先声》的文章，其中涉及组成以宣传民主思想为目标的新民党，以及提出以不合作方式进行公民行动的蓝色运动倡议等内容，被南京市警方刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被江苏省宿迁市中级人民法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江苏省南京市浦口监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，原南京师范大学副教授、南京著名人权捍卫者郭泉因关注湖北武汉疫情，为疫区人民发声而遭中共当局抓捕，随即被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，郭泉的母亲顾潇向媒体证实，郭泉本月中旬已经被南京检察院以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”批捕。南京警方指郭泉在网络上发表了国情及疫情等信息大<span lang="EN-US">500</span>篇文章，其中半数是在煽动民众。斯伟江律师<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在南京市第二看守所，会见郭泉。郭泉以煽动颠覆国家政权罪，在徐州市法院审理。对他指控，主要是微信上他的郭泉语录。郭泉满面红光，穿个短袖，身体健康。郭泉声言不惧坐牢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">郭秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">北京密云区不老屯镇雁洛村人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾先后三次被非法抓捕，其中两次被非法劳教。在劳教所，其虽受迫害，但仍坚持信仰，拒绝转化，拒写“三书”（保证书、决裂书、揭批书）。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其虽从山西省女子劳教所严管组被释放回家，但自此一直被当局视为重点“攻坚”对象，屡遭当地大队、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、派出所、司法部门的上门骚扰、威胁、逼迫写“保证”及恐吓威胁，使其全家的正常生活受到严重干扰，家人感到巨大的压力和恐惧。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，中共开“两会”期间，郭秀云去亲友家路上，再次被不老屯派出所警方绑架，并被非法抄家，拿走电脑、打印机、法轮功真相币等私人物品，并被关押在北京市密云看守所。其关押期间，因受迫害而导致身体很差，在第一次被法庭庭审时，竟昏倒在地，家人多次要求放人遭拒。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，其被北京市密云区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭延达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十一岁。被抓捕迫害前，在市内某大酒店当过厨师，因修炼法轮功，郭延达<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被营口市站前区东桥派出所警察从家中抓捕。警察抄走郭延达家的私有财产：电脑、打印机、钱、汽车及一些物品。现在被关押在辽宁省沈阳市第一监狱第二监区。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日辽宁省营口市站前区法院对营口市法轮功学员郭延达等庭审，后得知郭延达被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州市轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。锦州女儿河纺织厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，郭艳华和另两位法轮功学员在发放真相资料时，遭恶意构陷，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，送马三家劳动教养院。劳教期间，郭艳华被劳役、殴打，致使其头部受到严重损伤，郭艳华劳教期满回家后，她的精神状态变得很差，时而哭，时而笑，时而高喊，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月末在家被警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬，锦州市太和分局、锦州市太和区检察院、锦州市太和区法院沆瀣一气，判郭艳华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年刑期，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">果然： </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，北京市朝阳区人，陕西省西安市南郊大学城自由生意人，政治异见人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，因与友人经常在自己生意所在地聚会，自由讨论追求自由民主途径，被中共当局跟踪知晓，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年二人被西安市长安区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕刑拘，关押在西安市南郊三爻村看守所；之后因当局控其欲与他人密谋推翻中共政府，被西安市警方转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案被陕西省西安市中级法院庭审，终被以“颠覆国家政权罪”一审重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；另一人士亦被重判，但缺详情；据悉，因其平素做事隐秘，而当局对其审判亦不公开，故而对其入狱详情几乎鲜为人知，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日陕西省渭南市中级法院在网上发布了一份“果然减刑刑事裁决书”才得知晓，渭南监狱鉴于其在狱中有悔过表现，积分较多，建议减刑，但渭南市中级法院却以“屡次严重违反监规被处分”为由拒不减刑，依旧刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。目前在陕西省渭南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">H.</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><o:p></o:p></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈布力（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">哈哈尔麦<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿合曼（</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈萨克）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈里斯别克·巴班（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈木拉提•吾甫尔（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈纳提别克•萨布尔别克（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈伊拉提别克•木合塔尔汗（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">海莱提•尼亚孜（维吾尔）、海米提·阿不都热合曼（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郝劲松、郝明媚、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;">韩翠玲</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、韩建海、韩丽、韩猛、韩雪松、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩震昆</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杭霞、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何方美、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何观娇、何华、何菊英、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何莲春</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何萍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、何林夏、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何小兰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
