Roman&quot;;">贺桂珍、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贺云杰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑伊特</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洪桂连、洪柳、洪永忠、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">候井卫、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">侯巧珍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡宝龙、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡功、胡石根、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡水英</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、胡湘银、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡勇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡友刚、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡玉兰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、胡占亭、胡志琴、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄彪、黄春玲、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄根吉、黄红萍、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄建民、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄金桔、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄菊秀</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、黄连、黄俊娟、黄琦、黄信、黄秀兰、黄云敏、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄治萍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">哈布力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐县人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，新疆乌鲁木齐县哈萨克族清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰宗教领袖。因近来中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段，哈萨克族人也不例外，此间，因哈布力是乌鲁木齐县哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，并与海外宗教性事务多有交流联系，随遭地方当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年被乌鲁木齐县警方抓捕，后被乌鲁木齐县检察院正式批捕，控其“阅读及复印哈萨克斯坦国家宗教事务局的刊物”，违反了国家宗教问题的相关规定；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年被新疆乌鲁木齐县法院以不具名罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。据悉，当局对其如此重判是为了震慑新疆的哈萨克族人。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈哈尔麦<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿合曼：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区塔城地区沙湾县人，哈萨克族，前塔城地区东湾镇民族中学校长，前塔城地区沙湾县畜牧局党委书记，原塔城地区沙湾县第二中学校长，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于新疆塔城师范学院中专，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月毕业后又在新疆教育学院政治系进修大专，并于<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年毕业；曾常年在民族学校历任校长，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月曾任新疆塔城地区东湾镇民族中学校长，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年至被捕前，曾长期任塔城地区沙湾县第二中学校长等职；因工作敬业、成绩斐然，曾被多次被当地政府评为“先进个人”<span lang="EN-US">/</span>“双文明先进个人”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，突然被沙湾县警方以不知名罪由抓捕，并被送某教育集中营以接受“政治再教育”；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，获悉其已在同年早些时候被新疆塔城地区法院秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，</b>罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。目前被羁押地点或服刑监狱缺详。判刑之前其在被判刑前曾被迫认罪，家属遭软禁，探视权被剥夺，沙湾县纪委（中共纪律检查委员会）竟称如要让其释放，家属须交保释金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元人民币。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈里斯别克·巴班（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区昌吉回族自治州呼图壁县人，哈萨克族，新疆乌鲁木齐市居民，哈萨克民歌手，中国在押良心犯。身为一哈萨克族歌手，因喜欢传唱民族歌曲而深受亲友及当地民众的好评；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因曾到昌吉州吉木萨尔县泉子街镇吾塘沟村<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号参加表演，在表演会上演唱了“得罪中共当局”的歌曲，随遭到中共新疆当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“宣扬非法宗教等罪”抓捕，并被指控唱了政府认为“不该唱的歌曲”；据悉，自被捕后一直失联，家属不知其具体案情，只知至今尚未判刑，但又不被释放。目前被羁押于呼图壁县监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈木拉提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>吾甫尔</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：男，维吾尔族，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出生，研究生医学博士，“国家长江学者创新团队发展计划”发起者，曾任“新疆医科大学校长”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曾入选中国科学院院士曾选初步候选人名单，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月任新疆食药监局局长。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，最后一次在媒体上露面。现被证实，已被乌鲁木齐警方以“传播极端民族主义思想”罪由被抓，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，香港中文大学和声书院学生会发表声明，声援曾经到访学校的哈木拉提·吾甫尔。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被中共当局宣告「分裂国家罪」及「传播极端思想罪」成立，判处哈木拉提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>吾甫尔死刑，缓刑两年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈纳提别克•萨布尔别克（哈萨克）、哈伊拉提别克•木合塔尔汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">二人与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">海莱提•尼亚孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市人，原《新疆法制报》总编室主任、《法治纵横》杂志社副社长、《新疆经济报》前记者，原“维吾尔在线”网站的编辑和管理员以及维吾尔在线论坛版主，维吾尔著名媒体人，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，乌鲁木齐<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件后因多次接受包括香港《亚洲周刊》在内的采访，分析新疆骚乱的深层次原因，批评时任自治区书记王乐泉治理政策不当，并透露自己曾经在<span lang="EN-US">7.5 </span>前一天向新疆领导部门提出过预警却未被采纳等，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方从乌鲁木齐家中抓走，关押在乌鲁木齐天山看守所；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其家人收到当局的拘捕通知书，随后被乌鲁木齐法院以“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。现在新疆昌吉监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">海米提·阿不都热合曼（维）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Haimiti Abudureheman</span>，原伊犁州邮电局退休干部，中国在押良心犯。被捕前从未参与过政治维权或请愿活动，为人忠厚老实，深得其子女的爱戴及信任；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾与妻子沙阿呆提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>巴吴顿二人到土耳其旅行，并与已在瑞典流亡且参与政治维权和申请了政治庇护的儿子托格鲁克·海米提见过面，返回新疆时，因当时新疆并未出现“政治再教育营”之说，故其行踪随被当局知晓，但并未被伊宁市警方问讯或传唤训诫，就此二人一直相安无事；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年，随着中共当局在新疆出现大规模清理少数民族宗教文化行动以来，新疆各地越来越多的推出了“政治思想再教育营”（又称“政治再教育中心”）计划，其曾经出国探亲之举（即曾与成为政治难民的儿子见面），使其即刻变成当局仇视和需要严打报复的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其夫妇二人双双被伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市警方带走，并送某“政治再教育中心”羁押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，知其被伊宁市警方以“与在海外申请政治庇护的儿子会面”为罪由逮捕，近期被新疆伊犁州伊宁市法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日；</b>据悉，其在看守所内身体健康状况极差；其在乌鲁木齐市一家银行工作的女儿遭牵连，亦于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被强制送进“政治再教育中心”接受洗脑式教育，至今下落不明。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郝劲松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西“知名法律人士”。郝劲松生于<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年，山西忻州人。著名人权律师。郝劲松律师自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年开始先后<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次将国家税务总局、北京地铁运营公司、北京铁路局告上法庭，原他因对“打破行业‘霸王条款’起到了一定作用”而入选“<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年构建经济和谐十大受尊崇人物”。郝劲松被先后提名为<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法制新闻人物，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年度十大法制人物，并以“维权战士”的身份写入《<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法治蓝皮书》。因介入推动铁道部春运不涨价案件入选《<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国法治蓝皮书》，并当选<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国十大消费维权人物，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因介入陕西华南虎案件和杨佳案被《南方人物周刊》评选为“中国魅力人物——公义之魅”。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，介入上海“钓鱼执法事件”。后成立山西定襄县劲松法务咨询中心。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，郝劲松向定襄县环保局实名举报当地的诚泰纺织印染公司涉嫌污染空气和水源。郝劲松于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日就连续两天遭到户籍地山西省定襄县晋昌镇派出所以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日再遭该派出所传唤。随后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，行政拘留期满被转刑事拘留，控罪为涉嫌寻衅滋事。后遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，郝劲松在原先被控涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和诽谤罪之外，被加控诈骗罪，目前已经被移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郝明媚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">又名郝英吾，黑龙江省大庆法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十三岁，从事英语教师职业，原住黑龙江省北安市。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午，遭到大庆市公安局警察抓捕，后被以“利用邪教扰乱公共秩序”的罪起诉到大庆市让胡路区检察院，被批捕。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日判郝明媚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，并敲诈勒索两万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩爱珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省朝阳市龙城区下河首村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十六岁的韩爱珍，是位朴实忠厚的农村妇女。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚，韩爱珍与刘欣在粘贴大法真相时，被蹲坑的新华分局警察抓捕，并遭抄家，被关押在朝阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，韩爱珍被朝阳市龙城法院判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刘欣判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>缓<span lang="EN-US">5</span>释放回家。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩翠玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津法轮功女学员。因坚持向民众讲法轮功真相，韩翠玲多次被中共警察抓捕，曾三次被判刑。这一次被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月是她第四次被诬判。累计冤狱刑期<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日<a name="_Hlk54985393">韩翠玲</a>、邓桂秋、郭德芬三人，在天津市河西区九龙路万科广场（原世纪联华商厦）讲法轮功，被河西区桃花园派出所抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在天津市河西法院开庭。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩建海：男，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波<span lang="EN-US">,4</span>人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判韩建海<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，大学本科学历，籍贯海南省文昌市白秋二村。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。后获悉，韩丽被法院判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩猛<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后韩猛被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，韩猛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">韩雪松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市鲅鱼圈区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点，法轮功学员金翠香开着松花江小面包车，载着韩雪松（<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁）、韩美玲（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、柳爱敏（<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁）、徐笑岩行进在大连瓦房店李官镇的街道上，突然一辆警车拦截，随即围过来六七个警察，在车上搜出两小摞《九评》书。几名法轮功学员被抓捕到李官镇派出所。后刑拘逮捕起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日瓦房店法院判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员：金翠香<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩雪松被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩美玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；柳爱敏<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；徐笑岩、柳爱敏已获释。韩雪松刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩震昆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南昆明法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，原云南省网球运动队队员，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年转业到昆明锦华大酒店做服务员，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，因修炼法轮功被迫辞职。韩震昆因修炼法轮功，曾经两次被抓捕，入冤狱<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。此次是韩震昆自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年“<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">20</span>”中共迫害法轮功以来第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，韩震昆送<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名装修工人到西双版纳州景洪市，在装修工程完工，要返回昆明时，由于勐腊县勐龙镇景龙村中共党支部书记岩温恶意报警，景洪市国保警察以监控里怀疑韩震昆发放大法法轮功资料，在景洪东风农场永安宾馆内将韩震昆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，韩震昆被勐腊县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杭霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">合肥法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日杭霞被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开庭未判。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，合肥瑶海区法院近期到看守所向杭霞单独宣判：判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。不准上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何方美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日出生，河南省新乡市辉县人，网名“十三妹”，“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人，人权捍卫者。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，何方美年仅</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月龄的小女打了百白破疫苗之后导致全身瘫痪，其多方求助投诉均被拒，遂逐级维权讨说法，后因多地亦发生类似疫苗伤害宝宝事件，随组建</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体共同呼吁，以求当局关注并给予合理赔偿救治；然当局却对此一拖再拖，其被迫到北京上访，故屡遭抓捕打击。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，因中共两会期间与各地问题疫苗家长到北京王府井为残儿募捐，随被新乡市辉县警方行政拘留；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">21</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日又被以辉县警方转刑拘；关押期间因其拒绝认罪，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，被新乡市辉县检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕、起诉。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，何方美寻衅滋事案检察院以事实不清、证据不足撤诉，法院裁定准许，何方美已获释回家。出狱后，何方美继续为疫苗宝宝维权。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，何方美因欲赴北京给疫苗致残的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁女儿看病屡遭当局阻截，愤然泼漆当地政府牌子后，遭当局控制，已遭强迫失踪至今。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何观娇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，何观娇和妹妹何水姑到福州动车北站，买了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>号（大年二十九）早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分由福州北站来往北京西的动车。等待到第二天（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>号）早上离动车发车的前半个小时，何氏姐妹俩在福州火车站南广场，被一帮人共计六个人强行绑架到一辆白色私家车上。今年已经<span lang="EN-US">54</span>岁的何观娇，是上世纪七十年代因中越关系恶化而跟父母归国的侨民。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，何观娇分别在深圳市宝安区公明镇摩打制造厂和深圳市飞狮电子工业有限公司工作，因为长期接触有毒胶水，导致呼吸困难，多次昏倒，差一点死掉。何观娇多次要求用人单位调换工种被拒绝，加上得不到积极治疗，终失去劳动能力，被用人单位赶出厂门，到劳动仲裁部门要求进行工伤鉴定，被拒绝，遂开始了上访之路。由于何观娇在福州市晋安区新店镇横厝<span lang="EN-US">24</span>号<span lang="EN-US">20</span>座<span lang="EN-US">302</span>（福州北郊华侨塑料二厂）的房屋又遭强拆，且没有得到政府的任何安置，一直借住在姐姐妹妹家中。为了维护自己的合法权益，何观娇趁春节乘车方便，遂于大年二十九购买动车票，准备再次进京信访，却遭绑架失踪。后获知其被关在福州神康精神病院。在何水姑跟福州神康精神病院医生通电话过程中，被告知是公安将其强制送到精神病院的。至今仍未释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁的何华女士，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日向路人发送<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年新年挂历，被巡逻特警抓捕，先被关押在贵阳市云岩区拘留所，后转到贵阳市云岩区看守所。先判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后检察院抗诉，又于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日贵阳市中级法院又改判何华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何菊英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，湖南省宁远县人，湖南省宁远县中和镇上街村村民，维权访民，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，曾因其上初中的儿子被学校的几位恶少殴打致残，遭地方法院枉法判决，遂走上了漫长艰辛的维权之路；之后又因其上访的行为触碰了地方当局的利益神经，故而遭到地方当局的严酷打压，并因此屡遭非法关押；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾两次因上访维权遭遇政府枉法构陷，被先后处以劳动教养共计<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个月，并被多次关押于精神病院和黑监狱；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾因被关在教养所内，其家中老人无人照顾且遭到当局的恶意骚扰和恐吓，致使两位老人在惊吓过度和贫病交加中相继去世。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，当其再次到北京上访时，被地方当局从北京截访并强行遣回原籍，随后被警方以“非法上访”为罪由处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索政府罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被湖南省宁远县检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于湖南省宁远县看守所，后案件音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何莲春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省红河州蒙自市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年出生在石屏县宝秀镇，后嫁到蒙自县文澜镇高家村。此前<a name="_Hlk52323072">何莲春</a>曾接连两次遭冤判共<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年，在狱中熬过了<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，出狱后她到昆明打工，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份又被警察抓捕、构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。 何莲春<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，她与其他四名法轮功学员在蒙自城区贴法轮功真相资料时，被「<span lang="EN-US">610</span>」（专门迫害法轮功的非法机构）国保警察构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被红河州中级法院判重刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，提前<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，她再次被蒙自县「<span lang="EN-US">610</span>」抓捕到洗脑班「转化」迫害，由于她不放弃修炼，又被红河州中级法院判重刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。服刑期间何莲春曾遭酷刑虐待。在<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日何莲春被送入云南省第二女子监狱，关押在六监区期间，严管达五年多。期间，她被罚坐「小凳子」（长约<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多公分、宽约<span lang="EN-US">8</span>公分多），不准洗澡、洗衣，一天只给一瓶水（<span lang="EN-US">500ml</span>），近一年被限制次数上卫生间，而且经常遭到包夹（监管法轮功学员的刑事犯）的殴打、穿「紧束衣」、两次被开批斗会侮辱。何莲春进行了二十多次绝食抗议，遭到上百次野蛮灌食、灌药，饭食里投放不明药物。每次插胃管都是从她鼻子里硬插，导致她满鼻腔、满嘴都是血，每次她都要吐很多的血。由于插的次数多了，她的鼻腔、口腔、喉咙粘膜溃烂，吞咽非常困难。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月才刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，何莲春去探望法轮功学员王汇真，在返回住地的途中，被追到昆明来的蒙自市国保大队警察抓捕，说是为中共<span lang="EN-US">70</span>年「建国」阅兵维稳。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，她被建水县检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，何莲春被构陷到法院。她的所谓「罪行」是：她去看法轮功学员王汇真后，被抓捕时，一部手机被查获，里面存有法轮功资料。因此被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林松原市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午，何萍从母亲家回来，刚走进居民小区就被松原市国保大队抓捕、抄家。警察抄走电脑一台、真相手机五部、电话卡二十多张和所有大法书籍。后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。关押在松原市看守所一年之多后，现<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">何林夏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广西师范大学出版社集团前董事长，此出版社是大陆最先锋和最前卫的出版社，其打造的“理想国”、“魔法象”、“新民说”品牌也在读者和知识分子群体中享有很高的知名度。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广西检察院官方微信公众平台发布消息：日前，广西壮族自治区人民检察院依法以涉嫌受贿罪对广西师范大学出版社集团原董事长何林夏（正处级）决定逮捕，案件侦查工作正在进行中。据知情人士透露<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬何林夏就被逮捕了，与出版社年初计划出版已故历史学家高华的遗作和独立导演张赞波的作品《大路》被叫停有关，作为董事长的何林夏疑被秋后算帐。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，广西灌阳县人民法院以所谓贪污罪判处何林夏有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10 </span>年，这和其出版一些当局认为比较危险的书有关。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何小兰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。湖北浠水县法轮功学员。在中共对法轮功持续至今已有<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年的迫害中，她曾经被抓捕<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次，多次被骚扰、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午， 何小兰、袁明珠、张腊香、李婆婆，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位老人在一起学法，在浠水县公安局的“敲门行动”中被抓捕。李婆婆因家里有瘫痪病人需她侍候，关押到晚上释放，张腊香被关押了<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。何小兰、袁明珠分别被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何振宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆市万州区中学教师、法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。重庆市万州区甘宁镇中学<span lang="EN-US">18</span>级初二班主任和<span lang="EN-US">19</span>级初一数学教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，何振宇被抓捕。由于学校等方面援救两次，他被取保候审。但新一任校长换届后，由于何振宇不配合所谓的签字，他于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在学校外遭龙沙派出所抓捕，后被直接投入万州区看守所。后被直接判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何宗旺：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">福建省福清市的公民，长期致力于为弱势群体发声。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年在北京经营药材生意的他因为转发金水桥事件的帖子被刑拘<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年开始参与线下围观，<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>苏州拜祭林昭，到郑州旁听贾灵敏案庭审。两度赴庆安围观徐纯合案，期间被拘留十天。“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”系列案的潍坊案中被捕。潍坊看守所内遭受连续六天的疲劳审讯，关押近三个月后脊椎囊肿爆裂，导致下肢瘫痪且大小便失禁。潍坊看守所将其送院后，通知其家人取保接回福建老家治疗，留下后遗症。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，何宗旺在福州市第一看守所门口迎接刑满获释的严兴声时被抓捕，关押在福州市第二看守所。当局先抓捕再寻找罗织罪证，他们以何宗旺在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月闽清水灾过后进入灾区了解灾区情况为由，以“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪”执行逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月将其转往闽清看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，何宗旺被闽清法院以“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪、寻衅滋事罪”两个罪名分别判处<span lang="EN-US">2.5</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被福州市中级法院裁定：撤销原判 发回重审。代理此案的律师是广东的闻宇律师和山东的张金武律师。福州中院裁定原审部分认定事实不清、证据不足，发回闽清法院重新审理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，重审宣判：依旧<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贺桂珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">云南省昆明市老年法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1942</span>生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午四点左右，今年<span lang="EN-US">78</span>岁的贺桂珍，在发放真相资料时被摄像头监控录像，遭国保警察抄家。贺桂珍<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被转关到昆明市看守所。昆明市五华区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日上午在第十四法庭开庭庭审贺桂珍。贺桂珍遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被关押到云南省第二女子监狱。这是老人第二次被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贺云杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，贵阳市铁路客运段料库管理员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，贺云杰和刘淑娅为了帮助市民了解法轮功，发放法轮功资料，期间被人恶告。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，贺云杰和刘淑娅分别被贵阳铁路公安、南明区分局国保、二戈寨派出所警察抓捕、抄家，被关押到五当区三江看守所。被关押了<span lang="EN-US">162</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日分别被南宁区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑伊特：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑伊特于<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年在新疆喀什市出生，是著名的维吾尔族诗人及音乐家，擅长弹奏都塔尔琴，他的歌曲描绘维吾尔族历史文化，在土耳其也有知名度；他在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年创作《父亲》一曲，歌词提及「战争烈士」，后被抓捕。据悉其被中国当局认为是极端分子，在未经起诉下判囚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年。关押地点不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洪桂连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省计生牺牲品和政府不作为乱作为受害人。洪桂连因计划生育国策两次被黄山市屯溪区强制堕胎，此后唯一的儿子又因政府疏于安全生产管理，导致采砂船滥采滥挖河砂，导致家乡河道出现危险溺水而亡，为此洪上访维权，被迫接受政府所谓救助金，却被翻手为云覆手为雨的政府定为敲诈勒索罪。洪桂连出狱后申诉、控告无门，就赴京上访，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，从北京返家后的第二天就被警方以所谓网上逃犯名义抓捕，然后移交给安徽省黄山市警方，现在羁押于黄山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洪柳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆法轮功学员。母亲邓吉琼家住重庆市渝北区，林忠英家住重庆市巴南区。由于中共在法轮功学员的身份证上做标注，法轮功学员的正常出行时时受监控、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日一早，邓吉琼与未修炼法轮功的丈夫洪代鹏，乘高铁到成都。验票时，邓吉琼的身份证提示其法轮功学员的身份，邓吉琼和丈夫遭火车站人员拦截抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，邓吉琼亲家母林忠英也被抓捕，次日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，邓吉琼的儿子、林忠英的女婿洪柳被抓捕。他们被关押一年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，邓吉琼被重庆市江北区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，洪柳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，林忠英被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，三人同时被勒索罚金。洪柳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洪永忠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省海丰县人，广东省海丰县乌坎村民维权代表。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月曾因所在广东省海丰县乌坎村村民不满当局私自非法变卖村民土地，获利<span lang="EN-US">9</span>亿元且被村干部分摊，从而引发举世关注的乌坎事件，又因乌坎村民多次举行大规模维权游行示威，推行村民民主选举制度，并与警方数次爆发大型反抗冲突，遂遭广东当局的疯狂报复，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余人被抓、被通缉，其亦被广东当局定为“乌坎魏永汉、洪永忠等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人聚众扰乱社会秩序，非法集会、游行、示威，聚众扰乱交通秩序，妨害公务，故意传播虚假信息案”首要分子。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被网上通缉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬被陆丰县警方以涉嫌多种聚众扰乱社会秩序罪由拘捕，后转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日其案件在广东省海丰县法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被广东省海丰县法院一审以“非法集会、游行、示威罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“妨害公务罪”等多项罪名，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，控其“聚众扰乱社会秩序，情节严重，致使生产、营业无法进行，造成严重损失”。目前被羁押于海丰县公安局看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">候井卫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市通州区西集镇法轮功学员。侯井卫是<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被当地派出所抓捕、抄家，不法人员抢劫走大法书、电脑笔记本上台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台等本应该受法律保护的私人财物。其家人也被抓捕到派出所，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>天后家人被释放，但派出所派了一些村民监视侯井卫家人。侯井卫被关押在通州区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>侯井卫被通州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">侯巧珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北邯郸市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年已七十七岁，是邯郸市一位退休教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，侯巧珍与张培英在邯郸市复兴区彭家寨附近讲述法轮功被迫害真相时，被告发，遭复兴区公安分局彭家寨派出所抓捕，被关押在邯郸市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，邯郸市磁县法院在邯郸第三看守所里暗箱操作，对侯巧珍和张培英开庭，后判侯巧珍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，张培英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。侯巧珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡宝龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古通辽市蒙古族律师，通辽市蒙嘎立律师事务所负责人。胡宝龙毕业于内蒙古师范大学蒙文系，曾参与八九学运。后从事律师职业，胡宝龙曾代理内蒙古异议人士巴图张嘎案、著名蒙古族维权作家高玉莲案。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2010</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，胡宝龙被二连浩特边防警察禁止出境，理由是他涉嫌“危害国家安全”，并被告知其通辽市公安局已经把他列入到不能出境人员名单。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月底开始，内蒙古通辽市、鄂尔多斯市、呼和浩特市等多地的数万学生和家长发起罢课及抗议集会，反对当局加强汉语教学。胡宝龙是一名孩子的父亲，他不久前曾拒绝送孩子上课，并明确反对中共当局推行的“双语教育”活动，因此于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月初被通辽市警方刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被检察院批捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡功</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区人，原呼和浩特市回民区义和巷“芬芳理发店”理发师，曾被当地报纸誉为“<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年义务理发的好市民”，基督徒，呼和浩特市基督教“呼喊派”召会负责人，中国在押良心犯。曾因信仰有争议的基督教地方召会“呼喊派”，拥有“呼喊派”书籍，并与他人积极散发<span lang="EN-US">800</span>百余份福音宣传资料，触动了中共当局加强意识形态、信仰自由控制的敏感神经，随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被呼和浩特市玉泉区警方从居住地带走，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，被关押于内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市第三看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其涉嫌“邪教案”被内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区检察院提起公诉，被控以“小排聚会、主日聚会、婚礼聚会、境外特会进行聚集，通过电子邮件接收境外的邪教资料，与境外的邪教人员进行非法联系”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，最终被呼和浩特市玉泉区法院以“组织和利用邪教破坏国家法律实施”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日经呼和浩特市中级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判。目前具体服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡石根</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，江西省南昌市人，基督徒，北京基督教家庭教会圣爱团契、中原教会、雅和博教会长老，独立中文笔会关注会员，中国著名民主异议人士。<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月曾与王国齐秘密成立中国自由民主党，并参与康玉春等人成立的“中华进步同盟”；<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月曾与刘京生、高玉祥等人共同成立“中国自由工会筹备委员会”；<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月曾计划到北京、上海、武汉等地散发传单，并利用航模直升机在天安门广场空投传单，以抗议中共六四屠杀事件和纪念六四死难者，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被北京警方刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被以涉“组织、领导反革命集团罪”和“反革命宣传煽动罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被北京市中级法院以两罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，并在北京市第二监狱服刑，服刑期间身心因遭受巨大迫害曾一度病危，至<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被提前减刑获释。出狱后，因继续追求民主自由，关注、参与全国性劳工维权事件及公民活动，广结正义维权律师，又因笃信基督教而成为北京基督教家庭教会圣爱团契的传道人，遂一直遭当局传唤、软禁及强迫失踪等严打迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾因支持“中国茉莉花革命”而被警方秘押，并遭警方戴黑头套、殴打和威胁等；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日曾因参加“六四纪念研讨会”而被当局以涉“寻衅滋事罪”传唤，且被刑拘一个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日再次被北京警方传唤，自此失联，其家被抄，后得知其已于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被当局以涉“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被天津市警方正式逮捕，并关押在天津市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被天津市第二中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前在天津市长泰监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡水英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员胡水英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡湘银：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西宜春公民、残疾人胡湘银因积极参加维权行动<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被刑事拘留的，已于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被以诈骗罪批捕。胡湘银因为<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年介绍两位公民代理帮人打宅基地官司，当时因没达到对方要求（要四块地当地只给一块）。当事人因此恼怒告他们诈骗，后不了了之。后来在今年八月份胡因组织当地维权人士到上海声援一个被判刑的维权人士，结果被选择性“执法”抓捕。目前他家人生活困难也缺律师，需要援助。胡湘银是残疾人<span lang="EN-US">(</span>童年时双手被高压电击伤造成<span lang="EN-US">)</span>，靠开摩的维持一家五口的生计<span lang="EN-US">:</span>瞻养<span lang="EN-US">80</span>多岁的老母亲，抚养两个小孩<span lang="EN-US">(</span>最小的才满<span lang="EN-US">4</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">)</span>，尽管如此，他还是热心于公民维权，一有时间就积极参与维权行动。后获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖北钟祥市人，基督教华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）创建人及钟祥交通会骨干成员。曾因其与龚圣亮、徐福明等人共同组建基督教华南家庭教会，是湖北省荆门市钟祥市教会的骨干成员，并积极力促该教会在活动范围和信徒人数等方面迅速发展，随引起中共当局的极度恐慌和强烈不满，在把华南教会定性为“邪教组织”的同时，亦对其及其多名教会骨干成员施以严酷的打击；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因与徐福明等人一起被控涉嫌“参与<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在湖北省钟祥市对受害人谢东报复伤害案”，而被荆门市钟祥市警方以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被湖北省荆门市中级法院一审以同罪名判处死刑；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又经湖北省荆门市中级法院二审，以“故意伤害罪”改判为无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身。目前在湖北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡友刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省洮南市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，法轮功学员胡友刚、田超夫妇在洮南市的家被抄家，当天胡友刚被送入白城市看守所关押，田超被送入镇赉县看守所非法关押。胡友刚被关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>也底才得知被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，已于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被送至吉林省公主岭市监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡玉兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生，吉林市昌邑区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日发法轮功资料时，被街道人员报给昌邑区司法局，被抓捕、抄家，被关押在吉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日胡玉兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押到长春女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡占亭：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1949</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，辽宁阜新市人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因粘贴有关法轮功宣传信息，被辽宁省阜新市海州区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，曾因粘贴有关法轮功的真实信息，被阜新市海州区警方秘密跟踪抓捕，家被查抄，后被海州区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日其涉邪教案在阜新市海州区法院开庭受理，律师虽然为其做了辩护，但法庭却剥夺了胡占亭本人的辩护权，最终他被阜新市海州区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。其不服上诉，但阜新市中级法院却故意绕开律师，草草暗中非法宣判，维持原判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其被送到锦州监狱服刑，后于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日前又被秘密转监到沈阳市第一监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡志琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。胡志琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄彪：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1952</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，黄彪买东西回来，被国安蹲坑抓捕控制后抄家，警察抄走大量私人物品和几万人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日黄彪被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄春玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法、<a name="_Hlk54972260">黄春玲</a>、刘洪兰、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。黄春玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄根吉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛市即墨区田横镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，即墨公安局以将要召开青岛峰会“维稳”为借口，没出示任何证件，闯入黄根吉家抄家。后将黄根吉抓捕到即墨普东看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，山东省青岛市即墨区法院对黄根吉判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄红萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏启东市<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十一岁的法轮功学员，南京河海大学化学系八九届毕业生，原在启东盖天力制药厂工作，因坚持修炼法轮功，被单位开除，住南通市启东市寅阳镇临海桥村。黄红萍多次遭“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”（专门迫害法轮功的非法组织）与公安警察残酷迫害。黄红萍女士曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年出狱才几个月又被绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。近四年的迫害，致使她精神上、身体上遭受严重摧残，监狱医院诊断黄红萍得了宫颈癌。在南通监狱生命垂危。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，家属要求放黄红萍回家治疗，监狱负责人说，要写所谓“三书”才可以放人。所谓的“三书”就是悔过书、决心书、保证书。黄红萍表示坚修大法，决不写三书，目前在南通某医院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄建民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人。家住揭阳市东阳办事处东山村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，揭阳市榕城区公安分局国保大队伙同揭阳市东阳派出所，到黄建民家进行抓捕抄家。因黄建民在自己家开了商店，经常收到一些真相币，此次抄家抄到了真相币，就成了国保抓捕黄建民的冠冕堂皇的借口了。后黄建民夫妇被关押揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，<a name="_Hlk52321835">黄建民</a>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、妻子被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄金桔：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">她与赵文静、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后本案信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄菊秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南岳阳法轮功学员。从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共开始迫害法轮功学员开始到目前，黄菊秀被中共当局绑架已有<span lang="EN-US">12</span>次，并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次，曾被绑架到长沙捞刀河洗脑班强行洗脑迫害，还遭受药物迫害，被单位停发工资九年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，黄菊秀被阳市楼区公安分局国保大队抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被非法刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，由儿子担保“取保候审”。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被岳阳市楼区公安分局国保大队再次抓捕，关押在岳阳市第二看守所。期间，被关进岳阳市康复医院，遭受精神迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，黄菊秀被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>月，黄菊秀被关押到湖南省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">黄连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省湛江市雷州市纪家镇上郎村人，原纪家镇制板厂工人，法轮功学员。因控告前中共党魁江泽民发动迫害法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被广东省湛江市雷州市国保队长等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人绑架，家被查抄，搜走电脑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">4</span>部、录音机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>部及个人所有法轮功书籍资料等私人物品。被关押在雷州市看守所期间，因黄连绝食抗议，曾遭到强行鼻饲迫害，身体非常虚弱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，黄连的家人收到判决书，得知黄连已被湛江市雷州市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，二审维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄俊娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。家住武清区上马台镇王老庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，黄俊娟在善良的向百姓传法时被抓捕，关押在武清看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被武清法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金勒索一万元。黄俊娟不服，已上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄琦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">六四天网人权事务中心创始人、负责人。黄琦<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚于家中被带走，其义工蒲飞也失联。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许被来自棉阳、内江和成都南站派出所的警察<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人闯入家中带走。黄琦<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日生，中国四川人，黄琦毕业于四川大学无线电子系，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年成立了“天网寻人事务所”，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年设立“六四天网”网站。由于网站同时还登载各种批评时政的文章，引发中国当局的关注。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日即六四事件十一周年纪念日的前一天，黄琦被警察捕。在被捕近三年后，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，成都市中级人民法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处黄琦有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，黄琦刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，黄琦改组六四天网为中国天网人权事务中心。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年中国汶川大地震后，黄琦积极参与救灾活动，同时为地震中死亡学生的家长提供帮助，而且在网上撰文揭露“豆腐渣”工程。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，黄琦和天网人权事务中心两名工作人员吃饭时被几名身份不明的人强行塞进一辆汽车带走。后被控「非法持有国家机密」受到刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，黄琦以非法持有国家机密罪名被正式起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日成都市武侯区法院对黄琦案进行了宣判，法院以“非法持有国家机密档罪”，判处黄琦有期徒刑三年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日黄琦刑满出狱，现定居于成都。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日中共十八大六中全会前夜间与外界失联。后被证实遭随州国保强制传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，著名人权捍卫者、六四天网负责人黄琦被四川省绵阳市法院以“故意泄露国家秘密罪”及“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其中“故意泄露国家秘密罪”<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，数罪并罚执行<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。狱中身体境况极差，但当局不准保外就医。也不准其<span lang="EN-US">80</span>多岁母亲入狱见面探视。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄信：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省界首市拆迁访民。黄信与界首市其他访民于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初赴京上访，返回界首市家中于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察抓走，并被警方抄走家中的信访资料。当晚<span lang="EN-US">19</span>时黄信被界首市公安局决定以“涉嫌敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，送界首市看守所羁押。据悉黄信就房屋拆迁之事此前起诉界首市东城街道办事处的行政案件一审胜诉。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄秀兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曾用名黄秀梅，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，住商丘市睢阳区，个体业主。作为法轮功修炼者。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，黄秀兰女士在商丘市睢阳区香君路与凯旋路交叉口向一个路人发了一本<span
