lang="EN-US">2018</span>年的吉祥娃娃新年台历。此人叫任文珠，是睢阳区街道办事处工作人员。她诬告黄女士，先是打电话给社区主任，后叫来了商丘市新城公安分局警察和商丘睢阳国保大队警察。她一直跟踪黄女士陆陆续续叫了好多人，最后在几里地之外的县城里一个洗衣机维修店绑架了正在修洗衣机的黄女士并非法抄了她的家。连她的姐夫和孩子都没有放过，一并绑架到看守所迫害。公安警察在敲诈勒索了家人几万元钱后才放两个人回家，在此案中却被成为“证人”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">2</span>，河南商丘睢阳区法院对法轮功学员黄秀兰的进行了庭审。来自云南的维权律师出庭为黄秀兰女士做无罪辩护，首先对此次庭审检察院、法院故意刁难、为难律师拒不接受律师正规的合法手续，差点非法剥夺当事人和律师的辩护权深表遗憾。在法庭辩论过程中，律师逐条驳斥了公诉人的指控。随后几天法庭宣判，黄秀兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄云敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄云敏是新疆生产建设兵团农三师图木舒克市的退休法官，因帮助农三师农场职工维权，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被以“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”拘捕。黄云敏案曾于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在新疆生产建设兵团喀什农垦法院开庭。后获知黄云敏被转送“法律援助中心”接受所谓的思想教育。并未有判刑信息。后获知，黄云敏因替百姓维权获刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日黄云敏因会见时告知其妻子自己被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年遭当众殴打。新疆退休法官黄云敏至今家属拿不到判决书。他是因异议学者子肃案被关押的黄晓敏兄长。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄治萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市高坪区法轮功学员。自从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮大法以来，黄治萍多次遭到中共的残酷迫害。这之前，曾<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被抓捕到洗脑班迫害、被抄家不少于十次。一家人被抓捕、关押，遭受巨大的身体、精神、经济上的损失。黄治萍的丈夫王道德被迫害含冤离世；孩子生活在恐怖之中；姐姐被迫害成精神病，家中老人含恨离世。黄治萍<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在龙门菜市场被高坪区公安局国保警察抓捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被开庭，随后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">I</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">J</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">季桂珍、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">嵇书龙、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉白（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉力利•阿布都拉（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾国玺、贾艳玲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">嘉扬多吉（藏）、嘉央洛追（藏）、加尔肯别克·卡生巴依（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江兰英、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江荣欣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">姜凤丽、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜海英、姜淑娥、姜伟、姜野飞、姜志林、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蒋立宇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蒋雅晖、蒋亚绒、蒋湛春、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金翠香、金丽燕、金玉红、金芝、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">靳付章、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">景春、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鞠殿红、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鞠世淼</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">季桂珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，苏州市法轮功学员，家住苏州市高新区浒关开发区南庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点半左右，苏州工业园区娄葑派出所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>帮便衣，闯到季桂珍家的老旧屋子（苏州皮市街前庙巷<span lang="EN-US">7</span>姬庙弄<span lang="EN-US">5</span>号），实施抓捕、抄家。当晚，季桂珍被“取保候审”放回。之后，季桂珍被构陷到苏州市吴江区检察院、吴江区法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，季桂珍女士，被苏州市吴江区法院庭审，近日得知，季桂珍女士被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海民主维权人士，因“厕所革命”<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被上海市公安局浦东分局刑事拘留，现拘押在上海公安局浦东新区看守所，罪名是寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写上「大病治不起，习胖在撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时收，打倒共产党」等字句，称“用一个小时在厕所门后写字，能够让上万人看到”。随后遭拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>：<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分季孝龙被“寻衅滋事罪”案在上海市浦东新区人民法院第二法庭开庭审理。季孝龙因言获罪被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">嵇书龙 ：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏阜宁的环保人士。嵇书龙女士家乡苏北阜宁地区的地方政府官员，为了所谓的招商引资创政绩，从苏南引进被勒令关停的严重污染环境的有毒企业，继而动用各种违法手段，强行征用农民耕地之际，她带领村民抵制并到北京信访反映实情，请求中央对地方政府这种不可持续的发展予以制止。然而得到的结果是一次次的暴力截访，一次次的暴力侵害，及一次次的非法拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，已经在北京一年多没有信访，只是靠处理居民废弃垃圾而生存的嵇书龙，被访民出卖住址后遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在北京被劫回地方后，直到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日其儿子到阜宁县公安局询问，才得知被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，关押在盐城市看守所中。嵇书龙被以“寻衅滋事罪”构陷一案，自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在盐城市阜宁县法院开庭审理后，家属终于在满五个月后的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日收到一审判决。阜宁县法院作出长达<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的恶意枉法重判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉白（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：吉白，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉力利﹒阿布都拉（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆和田市伊里其乡嘎宗村治保主任<span lang="EN-US">,</span>哈萨克族人权捍卫者。因同村村民买麦提明﹒买吐松经常使用穆斯林方式祷告，被当地公安局指控有“非法宗教活动”之嫌，进而抓捕刑拘，吉力利﹒阿布都拉亦因此被当地公安局指控给“买麦提明﹒买吐松通风报信，让他逃跑”，属于政府认定的所谓“双面人”，所以二人同时被捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，二人同案均被判刑，买麦提明﹒买吐松被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，而吉力利﹒阿布都拉被新疆和田市中级法院重判<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4-5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾国玺：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，原籍甘肃会宁人，成都电子科技大学毕业以后在广东深圳外贸工作和安家，后以写电脑软件为生。与各地民运人士多有往来，行事低调，很少有人知道他的情况。曾联署过《零八宪章》和多个人权呼吁书。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日贾国玺遭山东省阳谷县公安局刑事拘留，罪名是“颠覆国家政权”。目前被羁押在阳谷县看守所。截至目前，其亲属知晓与否、律师是否已有介入等均情况不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贾艳玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">:5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">嘉扬多吉（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，是甘孜县色西底乡木西村人，遭捕前以放牧为生。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14&nbsp;</span>日独自在县城一条街道上开展了和平示威活动，声喊出“允许达赖喇嘛尊者返回西藏”、“西藏要自由”等口号，抗议中共的治藏政策，随即遭到公安拘捕。当局稍后要求嘉扬多吉的亲友们，前往甘孜县公安局登记电话和手机号码，并警告他们不得将此消息传出境外。后信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">嘉央洛追（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县人，阿坝县甲尔多乡孜郎寺僧人嘉央洛追，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年约<span lang="EN-US">35</span>岁。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜晚在马尔康县人民医院门前被当局拘捕。据信僧人嘉央洛追是因为在微信上撰写并发送涉及“敏感”内容的文章，而被中共政府拘捕。后信息全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">加尔肯别克·卡生巴依（哈）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆维吾尔自治区博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市人，哈萨克族，职业不详，哈萨克国移民，宗教人士，中国在押良心犯。已于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年退休，之前曾多次前往哈萨克国（以下简称哈国）；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，正式移民至哈萨克国；因协助其妻及其两名孩子也移民到哈国，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，从哈国返回中国时，被新疆博乐市当局以“传播宗教极端思想，鼓励新疆哈萨克族人移民哈萨克”为由送入“去极端化培训中心”羁押；后虽有暂短释放，但很快又于同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博乐市警方收监逮捕；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州博乐市法院以“煽动民族仇恨，民族分裂罪”、“宗教极端犯罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月</b>；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其逃往国外的儿子珠玛丹<span lang="EN-US">.</span>加尔肯别克因不堪父亲蒙冤入狱被判，被迫向哈萨克国总统、外交部及社会菁英们发出求助呼吁，以期能使其父尽快获救；另据悉，截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其家人尚未收到任何官方对其的刑事裁决通知书；其妻、女因此受牵连，妻子图尔逊古丽<span lang="EN-US">.</span>努尔海已于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被原退休单位博乐市达勒特镇中心小学停发退休金，女儿山山古丽<span lang="EN-US">.</span>加尔肯因帮其聘请、委托辩护律师，亦被送入“去极端化培训中心”羁押，至今失联。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江兰英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员江兰英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江荣欣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳法轮功学员，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。深圳法轮功学员江荣欣被非法关押已经<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年后，今据悉已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。江荣欣，原深圳邮电局正式职工，因坚持修炼法轮功被开除公职，并多次被非法抓捕、劳教、关洗脑班。江荣欣<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在惠东县被绑架，先被关押在惠东县看守所，后来被劫持到深圳宝安九围看守所，出现心肌梗塞、高血压症状，被送医院急救。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，江荣欣在深圳宝安九围看守所又出现心肌梗塞症状，血压很高，危及生命。家属与律师要求取保候审被拒，后江荣欣被转到深圳市第一看守所加重迫害。他们逼迫江荣欣吃药、强制洗脑、施压，被江荣欣拒绝。家人请律师先后多次去深圳市第一看守所看江荣欣，都被无理拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日在深圳宝安区法院被非法开庭。法庭未当庭宣判。今据悉已被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">姜凤丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁凤城市宝山镇法轮功学员。姜凤丽于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被抓捕，据家属说是丹东市公安局直接来抓人、抄家，清早去的，当时姜凤丽还没起床。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月家属得到消息，<a name="_Hlk52325858">姜凤丽</a>已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被关押在辽宁女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜海英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山东省高密市拒城河社区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，高密市密水街道拒成河社区法轮功学员姜海英在外讲法轮功被迫害的真相，被李家营派出所抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，已押到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜淑娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省莱西法轮功学员。原是山东省莱西市汽车站职工，她因坚持对法轮功的信仰被开除公职及遭受多种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日姜淑娥在做家政的户主楼下遭莱西国保李为魁等人绑架，关押在普东看守所，后被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">姜伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省朝阳市法轮功女学员。姜伟因为坚持真善忍信仰，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被非法劳教三年；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被非法判刑八年；期间她被迫离婚、遭受酷刑，被关精神病院，被摧残得了胃癌。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，姜伟再次遭绑架，半年后又被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">姜野飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川成都人，约生于<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年，民主人士，人权捍卫者，参加过“八九”学运，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年“汶川地震”后又积极参与维权活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年“六四”前夕，姜野飞在曼谷中共国大使馆门前参与纪念“六四”二十周年静坐活动，被泰国当局抓捕，关押近三年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日与董广平逃亡泰国，二人同被泰国警方在其持有联合国难民署签发的“庇护申请者证明书”（实为保护信）的前提下又以涉嫌“偷渡罪”抓捕，并关押于泰国曼谷市沙吞移民监狱；后经各方民主人士努力和紧急呼吁，被联合国难民署获悉，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日答应拟启动紧急通道，力促使其全家获准难民身份；但<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日仍被中共当局以“非法越境罪”遣送押解回国。于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被重庆公安局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”、“组织他人偷越国境罪”逮捕。目前羁押于重庆市第二看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，重庆市第一中级法院对姜野飞颠覆国家政权、偷越国境案宣判，认定姜野飞犯颠覆国家政权罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，犯偷越国境罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金一千元（人民币，下同），决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金一千元。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜志林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆博乐市访民姜志林下肢残疾，在博乐市务农。因自治区水利厅新水饮《<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>》<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号文件不落实，造成村民长期用水困难。姜志林为此逐级上访反映，均不但得不到解决，反而多次遭到威胁、殴打、拘留。之前姜志林因为举报村主任贪腐，被警方一再迫害打击，拘留多次，上访拦截抓捕，当地政府一直企图把姜志林构陷入狱。姜志林热心公益，经常以 “南国林子”的网名转发微博。他身残志坚，曾在小安妮失学事件中，大力呼吁网民关注，还不断为入狱的郭飞雄等良心犯呼吁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月据知情者透露：姜志林曾签字接受了当地有关基层部门每月一千五百元低保待遇，却被以“敲诈勒索罪”遭当地检察院批捕。姜志林是<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆博乐警方抓捕的，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被当地检察院以“敲诈勒索罪”逮捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蒋立宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原在北京一家教育机构工作。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚上，她和法轮功学员田丰及单珊，在北京街头张贴揭露“天安门自焚假案”的不干胶贴纸，被非法抓捕关押至今。据大陆媒体报导，蒋立宇、田丰及单珊分别被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蒋雅晖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">杨宏、蒋雅晖为夫妇二人，天津市南开区人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。二人均于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代起开始信仰法轮功，所以屡遭当局逼迫打压。杨宏原为天津丰田汽车发动机公司职工，为人心地善良、待人厚道、工作敬业肯干，公司领导因其工作成绩出色，特派他到日本深造。但自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始迫害法轮功始，他被单位突然召回，当局要挟威吓他要放弃练习法轮功。因拒绝放弃信仰，杨宏之后曾被非法劳教两次，累计刑期达<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，其身体受到严重迫害，瘦弱到只有<span lang="EN-US">70</span>斤。劳教期间，天津丰田汽车公司亦非法解除了与杨宏的劳动合同。蒋雅晖，系杨宏的妻子，为人单纯善良、待人真挚，因信仰法轮功而被天津当局劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。期间，曾因不放弃信仰而遭到酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，夫妇二人在家中突然被天津市公安局、南开分局、华苑新城派出所警方联手抓捕、抄家，当场搜走大量私人物品（含笔记本电脑、光盘刻录机、多台打印机等），后被以涉“邪教罪”逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，二人被天津市南开区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，尽管二人在法庭上都依法申诉无罪，三名律师也当庭做了有力的无罪辩护，夫妻二人仍各被南开区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">蒋亚绒</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：陕西省咸阳市人，陕西省风轮股份有限公司（原名国棉一厂）职工，维权访民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年因企业违规操作，造成工伤事故，致其右手伤残，却得不到应有的劳动保险和工资福利。其向法院申诉，不仅没有得到公正裁决审判，反遭各级司法部门勾结枉法裁决，且其家人（即其女儿、母亲、哥哥）也跟着遭殃，被非法软禁数月。因多次申诉无果，其被迫采取进京维权，但又遭到当局维稳意识的残酷打压。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾被咸阳市渭城区警方先后<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次关押在拘留所和看守所，甚至被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。拘留期间曾屡遭酷刑折磨、虐待、毒打，导致身患数种疾病，获释后又遭车祸暗害，险些丧命，身体遭到严重迫害摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，因在北京上访又被警方暴力执法，强行将其遣返，押回当地后又被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<a name="_Hlk507360521"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日</a>，因其到北京继续维权，又被截访软禁，直到<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其家属才知其被咸阳市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日其被陕西省咸阳市中级法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蒋湛春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省镇江市京口区的维权人士。因为在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年清明时到北京福田公墓祭奠杨佳，在“十一”维稳时，被公安以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”指定监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年的最后一天，蒋湛春被第二次指定居所监视居住，被延长监视居住。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年清明节前夕<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日律师会见了蒋湛春，已经接到了起诉书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日已开庭。仍未判决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金翠香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市鲅鱼圈区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁的金翠香女士，原为辽宁省四七五化工厂<span lang="EN-US">302</span>车间工人。她却因坚持信仰法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，在冤狱中遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点，法轮功学员金翠香开着松花江小面包车，载着韩雪松（<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁）、韩美玲（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、柳爱敏（<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁）、徐笑岩行进在大连瓦房店李官镇的街道上，突然一辆警车拦截，随即围过来六七个警察，在车上搜出两小摞《九评》书。几名法轮功学员被抓捕到李官镇派出所。后刑拘逮捕起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日瓦房店法院判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员：金翠香<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩雪松<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩美玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；柳爱敏<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；徐笑岩、柳爱敏已获释。金翠香刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">金丽燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，福建省宁德市法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，金丽燕与肖传雄、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、庄友布、陈开奇、林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月其被取保候审，后因其继续从事法轮功宣传活动，又被收监逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，金丽燕被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省七台河市法轮功修炼人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初因去哈尔滨看望同修家孩子（同修因依兰县国保半夜上家砸门从窗户跳落时绳索断裂至死）时，在校门口被埋伏的依兰县国保抓走，现行政拘留后刑事拘留。期间律师一直未获得会见。当时律师向住所检察室反应情况，检察院住所检察室主人也配合看守所撒谎说人不在看守所了，也不告知人是释放了还是被哪个办案机关转移走了。因为疫情原因，案子<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号经过检察院两次退补后送到了法院。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月金玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">金芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。金芝<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年四十九岁。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。金芝于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上出门去打工，在自家楼下遭到抓捕，十几个警察一拥而入闯进金芝家中非法抄家。此次行动为天津市公安局、北辰分局、瑞景派出所联合出动实施的抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月末，金芝被天津北辰区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">靳付章：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年四十一岁，家住辽宁省营口市西市区，是一公司的优秀职员，因他坚信法轮功，一九九九年七月后被非法关押迫害<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，营口市公安局站前区公安分局国保大队组织站前区东风派出所警察将在家中的靳付章抓捕，并抢走法轮功书籍、笔记本电脑、自家车等许多私人物品。靳付章被关押在营口市看守所，成天被迫做奴工，吃不饱，干着打磨锡纸有害身体健康的活。营口市西市区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月对他庭审。当庭没有宣判。后得知，靳付章被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在大连监狱第五监区（地址是：大连市甘井子区姚家街<span lang="EN-US">300</span>号<span lang="EN-US">3-3 </span>）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">景春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，吉林省盘石市人，吉林省盘石市安乐乡村民，维权冤民，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因与同村另一村民发生的一次冲突而被警方于次年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日刑拘，并关押在盘石市公安局东山看守所，遭受严刑拷打；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被当地法院利用虚假证据，在未开庭的情况下，以“故意伤害罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，赔偿伤害人医药费<span lang="EN-US">1711.97</span>元；后经其妻刘金艳多次维权上诉，法院才不得不改判其无罪，并于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日将其释放；获释后，因其就被枉法关押一年一案依法向法院提出国家赔偿申请，遭到法院无理拒绝，遂被迫走上漫长艰辛的维权之路，期间多次遭遇到地方当局的打击与迫害，身心俱损；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年底，因其再次向当地政府提出信访诉求，随被 盘石市警方于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日强行抓捕，并以涉嫌“敲诈勒索（政府）罪”被刑拘，关押于吉林省盘石市看守所；一个月后，又被以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被吉林省盘石市法院宣布重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，经二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。目前在吉林省长春市宽城区兴业监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk507375253"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">鞠殿红</span></b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，<a name="_Hlk507370737">鞠殿红</a>因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鞠世淼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，辽宁凤城法轮功学员，原辽宁省直信息总台财务人员。为修炼法轮功，鞠世淼曾多次去北京上访，曾被拘留，劳教，合计<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，丹东市凤城市法轮功学员鞠世淼、孙忠琴、佟秀红，在凤城大兴镇，给村民送明慧新年台历、福字和期刊等，被大兴镇政法综治委员宋传刚等人抓捕，后被构陷到丹东市振安区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被丹东市振安区法院判刑：鞠世淼被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；孙忠琴<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；佟秀红<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。佟秀红于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被“取保候审”，已回家。鞠世淼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">K</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卡姆巴尔•阿穆巴尔大毛拉（维吾尔族）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阚光英、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">康艳玲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柯昌炎、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肯杰别克﹒阿纳尔别克（哈萨克）、肯杰别克•达列力（哈萨克）、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孔庆艳、孔文涛<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">卡姆巴尔<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿穆巴尔大毛拉（维吾尔族）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆和田市哈尼埃里克镇人，维族名<span lang="EN-US">Qamber Amber Damolla</span>，新疆维吾尔族著名宗教学者，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在新疆和田市哈尼埃里克镇高中曾有<span lang="EN-US">17</span>名维吾尔族人被中共和田市当局抓捕，指控他们的言行涉及了与国家安全有关的各种罪名，卡姆巴尔<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿穆巴尔大毛拉亦是其中之一。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获悉，其终因不与中共新疆当局合作，而被新疆和田市中级法院以“危害国家安全罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阚光英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省安康市法轮功学员，女，五十四岁，个体经营户。一九九七年秋修炼法轮功。阚光英因修炼法轮功，多年来屡遭残酷迫害，长期被监视居住、监控电话，先后七次被抄家、三次被拘留、被劳教二年、被判刑四年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日阚光英在自家商店被抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并被罚金五千元。至今阚光英已被关押一年多，看守所从不让家属接见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">康艳玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。康艳玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柯昌炎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年出生，大湖北省黄石市冶茗山乡上汪村大楼家冲法轮功学员。自中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月迫害法轮功以来，柯昌炎曾多次被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日在北京上访，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，，遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在家被抓捕，再次被关押在湖北省沙洋劳教所迫害<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日清晨，茗山乡派出所警察闯入柯昌炎家中，抓捕后才通知家属，也没有出示任何证件，将柯昌炎关押在大冶熊家边拘留所。被非法关押构陷一年多，得知被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被迫害的只有皮包骨，并于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被押到湖北省沙洋监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">肯杰别克﹒阿纳尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年龄不详，新疆博乐市人，哈萨克族，异见人士。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，因其从哈萨克斯坦国探亲回国后，在微信群里转发了一些移民哈萨克斯坦国的信息，发表了相关言论，并协助本村村民移民哈萨克斯坦国，被当地警方知晓，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被新疆博乐市警方以</span><span style="font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: &quot;MS Mincho&quot;;">​​​​</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">“</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出卖国家机密罪”为罪由拘捕，之后一直失联；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被新疆维吾尔自治区博乐市法院一审以“泄露国家秘密罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前被关押于新疆博乐市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">肯杰别克•达列力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孔庆艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、赵兴有、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孔文涛，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">66</span>年生，江苏南京人，副主任医师，南京高淳区人民医院消化内科主任，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年毕业于南京医学院，堪称南京本地的名流望族。因追求民主宪政，期望建立一个法治国家，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初被当局逮捕，今天有消息传来，孔文涛被以颠覆国家政权罪判刑十三年，当庭认罪，且不上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>
</div>
